The date of the reception for representatives from various medical associations will be from the morning of December 30, 22nd year [1933], to noon on January 4th, 23rd year [1934]. We especially send this letter so you may know that all members apart from the representatives of your association are welcome to attend freely in Nanjing. Please also indicate the members' names on the list that will be sent to us so that we can arrange the seats in advance.

Ziyou Association Conducting Relief for Street Children – Forming Investigation Groups – Giving Popular Lectures

The Chinese Youth Association believes that the number of street children has been increasing, begging in the streets, living an unsettled life, dirty and ragged, and prone to laziness. Charitable organizations are unable to accommodate them. If other paths are not opened up to provide relief, they will inevitably become thieves, which is unimaginable for the future of society. In view of this, the association has dispatched personnel to actively investigate and has organized the already investigated street children into groups to carry out work, with regions as units. The details are as follows:

Zonal Investigation

The association has dispatched specialists to investigate street children in various locations, and then form groups, with zones as units, such as the Taikoo Wharf team, the North Railway Station team, the Sichuan Road Bridge team, etc., to investigate separately, in the hope of completing the task as soon as possible, so as to find ways to provide relief and avoid becoming vagrants.

Causes of Vagrancy

It was found that among the street children, there were (1) 23 who had been displaced by disasters such as floods, fires, soldiers and bandits, or because their fathers or brothers had committed crimes; (2) 11 who had escaped because they did not study and were beaten by their fathers or brothers; (3) 8 who had escaped because they were apprentices who did not work hard and were beaten by their masters; (4) 13 who had escaped because they had been lured by their peers; (5) 2 who had escaped because they were addicted to gambling and lost money; (6) 40 who were begging because they were poor and had no food or clothing; (7) 3 who were soldiers who had been laid off. Among these 100 people, 69 were willing to enter the association's educational institute, and 31 were willing to remain vagrants for the rest of their lives.

Providing Education

The association plans to give the one hundred or so street children popular lectures and entertainment, to cultivate their character, so that they can be subtly influenced and brought back on the right track. However, those who are of good character and have lofty aspirations will be given appropriate education. If they are sick, they will be sent to the association's hospital for treatment.

Unemployed Man Commits Suicide Due to Poverty

Yue Guisheng, a native of Suzhou, 21 years old, used to work as a butcher at the Su-Xi Zaisheng Company at No. 50 North Chengdu Road. Because he was not working hard, he was laid off by his employer. After Yue lost his job, he stayed idle at home. The afternoon before last, at about 4 p.m., Guisheng, because of economic pressure and the difficulty of living, suddenly had the idea of being tired of life. When no one was looking, he swallowed a yuan's worth of raw opium. Later, he was discovered by his family and rushed to the Longhua Hospital. However, because he had been poisoned too deeply and treatment was too late, he died early yesterday morning. His body was sent to the autopsy room for examination.

Zhongfu Silk Mill Increases Capital and Expands

The Zhongfu Silk Mill has been operating for nearly ten years. Initially, it was planned to raise 500,000 taels of shares. However, because silk was a newly established industry and few were interested, it opened for business after only half of the shares were collected. In just a few years, the results were significant. In addition to all the additions, repayments of start-up costs, and deposits of new and old public reserves, shareholders were still able to distribute 1.34% of official dividends annually. In addition, boilers and machines were surplus, in order to expand the base for further step-up in Japan, all that was lacking was a spindle. Recently, due to the daily decline in silk prices, it was necessary to increase output and reduce costs to add looms to fundamentally solve the problem. A temporary shareholders meeting was held on the 7th of this month, and it was decided to increase capital by 150,000 yuan. Each share was changed to 100 yuan. Shareholders have enthusiastically subscribed. However, for the sake of promoting interest in investment in industry, it was decided that 150,000 yuan would be taken up by old shares, leaving 100,000 yuan for investment from all sectors, with the aim of sharing benefits equally. It is said that the deadline for payment is the end of the Western calendar year.

Magnificent Opening of Furen Hospital

The opening of Furen Hospital on Mintiniyin Road in this port took place the day before yesterday (the 9th). The reporter went at ten o'clock and was personally greeted by Mr. Shen Liuchun, a director of the hospital. The hospital's internal facilities are complete, such as electrotherapy, sun lamps, X-rays, through-flow electricity, steam baths, etc., far superior to ordinary hospitals. Even the ward equipment, from special class to third class, is very clean. Hot and cold water pipes and water radiators, as well as bathrooms, are available. Patients can call the hospital staff not with an electric bell, but with a red light, to avoid noise. This shows the depth of the hospital's intentions. Great doctors Xie Qigang, Zhu Baoliang, and Zhou Jifu are all deeply skilled in medicine and agile in surgery. Those who are poor and sick and seek medical attention and have a reliable guarantee will only be charged a fee to cover food expenses. Over two hundred guests attended, including business tycoons Yu Qiaqing and Sun Meitang. Yuan Ludeng and Fang Jiaobo each presented congratulatory inscriptions. The hospital specially prepared Western pastries to entertain the guests. Everyone was happy and dispersed at around four o'clock in the afternoon.

Apprentice Zhu Yusheng Arrested for Absconding with 5,000 Yuan – Bankbook for 4,800 Yuan Seized

Mao Zhonggang, manager of the Jutai bean and food store at No. 24 Dongjiadu, Nanshi, instructed his apprentice, Zhu Yusheng, 19 years old, from Wusong, on September 12th of this year, to take 5,000 yuan in paper money to deposit at the Huixiangzhuang in Jixiang Lane, French Concession. Unexpectedly, the apprentice Zhu Yusheng had ill intentions, absconded with the money, and never returned. Store manager Mao Zhonggang, knowing that he had absconded with the money, separately reported the case to the Chinese and Concession authorities and requested that a general order for arrest be issued. Lu Ying, captain of the Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau Detective Team, had already issued a general order to all precinct detectives to rigorously investigate and arrest him. Yesterday afternoon, at around 8 p.m., store employee Cui Guanqun went to a rice industry tea party in the North City for business. When he passed the intersection of Wai Xinqiao Street in Jiu Mu Di (Chinese territory), he ran into the apprentice Zhu Yusheng. He immediately stepped forward, shouted for the police, and arrested him, taking him to the First Precinct of the Second District for questioning. After the precinct chief clarified the circumstances, he ordered Inspector Xu and Liu Shaoqing, the detective team leader from the Second District General Office, to lead the criminal Zhu Songqing to the French Concession with Bao Detective Qin Youde from the Songshan Road Patrol Room, to his residence at No. 8 Xixi Lane, Maren Road, Route Lafayette. On the spot, they seized the original stolen bankbook for 4,800 yuan and took it to the Patrol Room. After questioning, they were brought back to the First Precinct of the Second District for questioning. He also confessed that he had gone to Beiping on September 13th to hide, but because he was not used to the food, he returned to Shanghai. He had spent dozens of yuan on travel expenses and paying tuition fees at a certain school. Zhu's guarantor, Jiang Hongbin, was also summoned to the case and briefly questioned. At noon yesterday, they were sent to the Third Section of the General Office for questioning.

Funeral for Madam Lu Liankui Scheduled – Venue Chosen as the Chinese Merchant Villa

After the death of Madam Zhang, the beloved wife of Mr. Lu Liankui, inspector of the Public Works Department Police Force in the Public Concession, the dates of the 1st, 2nd and 3rd of December, Western calendar (or the 14th, 15th and 16th of the Lunar calendar) has been set for the wake. Because Mr. Lu has an outstanding reputation and wide-ranging connections, it is expected that many military and government officials, gentry, merchants, and people from all walks of life from this port and other places will come to pay their respects. The old site of the Chinese Merchant Villa on Wenshi Lin Road has been chosen as the ceremonial hall. The building there is very spacious, with five courtyards. The main gate faces Wenshi Lin Road, and the side gate is on Haining Road. The depth and magnificence of the architecture are rarely seen. It is heard that one hall will be arranged as the ceremonial hall, where the portrait of Madam will be worshipped. Because Mr. Lu believed that simply displaying a framed photograph would not be spectacular enough, he decided to have a larger portrait specially made, with its appearance and smile as true to life as possible, so that those who admire her would feel as if her voice and appearance were still present. It is also planned that after the wake, the portrait will be moved back to the native place and placed in the ancestral hall for perpetual remembrance. In recent days, because the Chinese Merchant Villa has been unoccupied for a long time, the interior has been covered in cobwebs and dust. Craftsmen are being hired to repair and clean it thoroughly. As the main gate was not previously opened, it is considered inelegant, so it is waiting for the interior to be cleaned up before the main gate will be repaired. There are only three weeks left until the wake, so there is plenty of time to make preparations. It is expected that the scene of plain carriages and white horses will be even grander than on the day of the funeral.

Fire at Zhixiang Type Factory

At nine o'clock in the morning before last, a fire suddenly broke out at the Zhixiang Type Factory at No. 6 Huacheng Road in the French Concession. Flames soared and sparks flew in all directions. Fortunately, the neighbor was the Qingyun Soda Fire Extinguisher Distribution Office. Guo Qingyun, the owner of the office, carried a self-made Qingyun soda fire extinguisher and sprayed it, the foam like mist, and extinguished the fire in a moment. By the time the fire brigade from the Songshan Road fire station arrived, there were no traces of fire. The loss was very small, only burning some boards and several frames of lead type. After the incident, the police department ordered detectives to investigate and summoned the owner of Zhixiang, Mr. Lu, to inquire about the cause of the fire.

Car Kills Police Officer

The Rue de Gênes in western Shanghai is located in the Chinese-administered area. The Sixth District Public Security Bureau has set up guard posts there to maintain order. At approximately 5 PM the day before yesterday, a rickshaw puller reported to the nearby guard that a person dressed as a policeman had been run over by a car on Zhongshan Road and was dying. The guard rushed to the scene and found a colleague. Upon closer inspection of the uniform, he was identified as Chu Enxue, a police officer from the Tianbao Lane Police Station of the Fourth District. The guard immediately hired a car to take him to the Red Cross Hospital, but the rescue was ineffective, and he died shortly after. As for the car that caused the accident, the area was sparsely populated, and no one noticed it, so it escaped without a trace. Afterward, the guard reported the incident to the Sixth District Headquarters, which relayed the information to the Tianbao Lane Police Station by telephone. According to the patrol officer, Chu had requested leave that afternoon at 3 PM for personal matters and left, destination unknown. It was deeply regrettable that he was struck by a car and died two hours later.

Predicting the Great Whale's Travels

The great whale, weighing 100,800 catties, which was exhibited in Shanghai, has concluded its exhibition after more than six weeks. It is now planned to transport it to Shandong and Hebei provinces, as well as the Tianjin and Beijing areas. The railway car carrying the whale has already been sent to Wusong for repairs so that it can be transported via the Jinpu Railway. The first stop will be Jinan, where it will be displayed for about two weeks, followed by Tianjin and Beijing. Then, it will return to Shanghai, with planned exhibitions in various locations along the Jinpu and Jinghu Railways, totaling about six months. It is understood that the Tai'an Orphanage has obtained the rental rights from the whale's owner to use the exhibition revenue to help the millions of children who have been left homeless by the Yellow River floods. The orphanage has a proven track record of excellent work in the past, and this new method of saving disaster victims will greatly benefit the country.

Missing Young Girl from Changzhou

Mrs. Zhang Wang from Changzhou brought her young daughter, Rongguan, to Shanghai on the ninth of this month to visit relatives. German Sports Expert Georg Kibel to Visit China

German sports expert Georg Kibel recently sent a letter to Mr. Liu Xuesong, stating that he will be visiting Shanghai soon. Mr. Kibel was sent by the German government to the United States to study sports. He is now returning to Germany from the United States and will be touring East Asia along the way. He will first visit Japan, then Beijing and Tianjin, and is expected to arrive in Shanghai around the 12th of this month. It is said that Mr. Kibel is one of the members of the preparatory committee for the 11th World Games to be held in Berlin in 1936. When Mr. Liu was in the United States last year, he often worked with Mr. Kibel at the World Games and became good friends. This time, he is coming to China to study the current state of sports in our country. He will stay in Shanghai for several days and then go to Nanjing to visit important figures in our government. The YMCA in Shanghai is preparing to invite him to give a lecture, and the German consul in Shanghai is also preparing a welcome reception.

Fifth Municipal Elementary School Games Track and Field Competition Reaches Final Stage Today: Too Many Events, Starts Early at 8:30 AM. All Events Conclude Today, Awards Ceremony to be Scheduled

Yesterday was the second day of the fifth annual municipal elementary school joint sports meet. The weather remained good. All events will conclude today. However, due to the large number of events, the competition will start early at 8:30 AM. All judges, staff, and male and female athletes from each school must arrive on time. The details of yesterday's competition are as follows:

Sports Overview

Group Exercises

Yesterday, a total of fifty-five group exercise routines were performed, such as Bide's shield exercise, depicting the Sino-Japanese War, Shanghai Shangxue's colored flag exercise, with various patterns, Qunshihui's deaf-mute exercise without commands, Tangwan Elementary School's lower grades' "baby soldiers," with their tender legs fully exposed, Youlong's dragon dance with graceful poses, and Lin Yin's character exercise, forming the eight characters "Lin Yin Elementary School Reading to Save the Nation," which was particularly commendable. Other excellent performances included Caotang's freehand exercises, He'an's short stick exercises, and Haozhu's vaulting box performance. The Shanghai Kindergarten's "little workers" and Minzhi's "little farmers" embodied the meaning of production education. Longde's national flag exercise, Tangwan's rice harvesting dance, and Qunxuehui's "little heroes" were particularly interesting.

Track and Field

The track and field competition yesterday completed the finals for the men's groups' shot put and the A group's high jump and long jump, as well as the women's A group's 100-meter dash, etc. The men's groups' 100-meter dash has also entered the finals stage. However, no new records have been set in the past two days. Wan Zhu's Zhu Hongqi's long jump result of 5.46 meters in the men's A group was close to the record held by Jia Youliang. The men's A group 800-meter preliminary was originally a highlight, but it started at five o'clock, and it was difficult to see clearly in the twilight. In the men's 100-meter A group final, the results of Xicheng's Hu Kaihou and Shanghai North's Cao Jiabao were close, and there is sure to be intense competition.

Sidelines

The Security Team is Very Busy

The South District Security Team was very busy on the field, providing service. Outside the sports field, at the students' rest area, many vendors were selling spiced beans and peanuts. Many elementary school students were hungry and scrambling to buy them. However, the sale of goods by vendors was not allowed by the regulations, and the security team members were running around, grabbing one after another, which was quite amusing. The Guanshengyuan food stall was specially permitted to be set up and was not subject to the ban, so business was booming.

Weigh-in Area: Athletes Disarm

In the track and field competition, the authorities of each school were eager to win and often did not follow the regulations, with the A group pretending to be the B group, and the B group pretending to be the C group. Especially in the track events, tall people were often found impersonating others to win championships in the C group. The judges did not let their guard down and reweighed them, finding that they all weighed over 80 pounds, and their qualifications were revoked. The weigh-in area was bustling for a while. The elementary school students were very clever, taking off their outerwear and running barefoot at the time of weighing, but the difference was limited, and they still returned disappointed.

Bizarre Costumes of Kindergarten Students

The costumes of the kindergarten students from each school were colorful and ingenious. The most aristocratic was the Wanzhu Kindergarten, with costumes made of red and black silk velvet. Xicheng and Shangwen had specially made national wool sweaters from Yansheng Industrial Society, which were also quite modern. The most simple were the Minzhi Kindergarten students performing as "little farmers," wearing blue silk cloth farmer's clothes on the upper body, a homespun apron on the lower body, a bamboo hat on the shoulder, and straw sandals on the feet, looking like real farmers, which was very special.

Qin Zhixue is a Standard Beauty

Ms. Qin Zhibao, the physical education instructor at Wanzhu Elementary School, graduated from the Southeast Women's Physical Education College. She has been teaching at Wanzhu for many years and has participated in three elementary school sports meets in a row. Her muscles are fair and firm, with the style of Xu Lai. The crowd calls her a "standard beauty." In the morning, she wore a coffee-colored cheongsam and leather shoes. When she exercised in the afternoon, she changed into a white sports shirt, which was shining brightly, with a line of English characters on the hem. Her thighs were revealed under the short skirt, truly a sports athlete.

This year's International Walking Race is scheduled for December 10th. According to the race committee's announcement, the committee will pay special attention to the posture of the racers this year. The movements of the toes and heels must strictly comply with the rules.

Youth Handball Ranking Tournament: Yan Zhaorong Promoted to 8th Grade

Yesterday's youth handball match was between Lu Mengsheng and Yan Zhaorong. In the first game, Lu took the lead and scored eight points in a row. Although Yan tried his best to catch up, he failed. Later, the scores of the two were extremely close. At 19 points, Yan finally caught up and tied, and surpassed him to win the final victory with 21 to 19. In the second game, Yan won with a single effort, winning with 21 to 3, and jumped to the eighth grade. Today at 3 pm he will play against the seventh-ranked Gao Zishou.

The National Games Closed Many Days Ago, Qinghai Athletes Arrive in Beijing Late: Encountered Rain and Robbery on the Way, Experienced Hardships and Arrived in Beijing Late

After the closing of the National Games, Qinghai athletes Zhang Shengzhu, Ma Si, Wu Yongtai, Wang Tingzhang, and team leader Zhao Yongjian left for Beijing on the 9th of this month to deliver a report from Ting Xiyao, Director of the Education Department, to the Ministry of Education. It is reported that in addition to the 13 athletes who came to Beijing last time, there are still these five people from Qinghai. Because they set off in two groups, these five people started from Qinghai on September 11. They encountered rain, and the ground was muddy and inconvenient for cars, so they walked on foot. They also encountered bandits and took detours. After experiencing hardships, they arrived in Beijing late today. National Games staff member Liu Yabai accompanied the athletes to visit the Central Sports Field. Guo Lianfeng went to the Ministry of Railways at the request of the athletes to ask for special accommodation for the five people and issue free tickets back to Qinghai.

13-Mile Open Walking Race to Be Held Tomorrow Morning: Women's One-Mile Walking Race to Be Held at the Same Time; 198 Men and Women Participants

The 13th Men's 13-Mile and 2nd Women's 1-Mile Walking Race, which has been widely publicized for more than a month, is scheduled to be held at 8 am and 10 am tomorrow, respectively, rain or shine. The number of men and women participants is very enthusiastic, reaching 198 people. This is also due to the enthusiastic assistance of various circles and sports associations. It is reported that the male athletes must gather at the starting point (Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road intersection) at 7:30 am, call the roll and line up at 7:45 am, and start at 8 am. They will return to the Chinese Athletics Field on Laorenfu Road and run one more lap around the track, a total of 13 miles. The guides are divided into two sections because there are too many participants. No. 1 to No. 70 will join at the intersection of Bailinan Road and Yuyuan Road, that is, in front of the Zhaofeng Garden, as the first section. The second section will join from No. 71 to No. 140 at the intersection of Wujiaochang Quejisi Road and Bailinan Road. Everyone must go to the designated location in advance to wait until they enter and exit at the intersection of Kangti Road and Lüban Road, and enter the west gate of the Chinese Basketball Hall at the intersection of Lafayette Road and Malang Road. To facilitate the competition of the athletes, the sixth-grade students of Tonghui Elementary School are specially requested to hold flags every mile to show the public. As for women, they run four laps around the track in the athletic field, a total of one mile. Roll call at 10:45 am, competition at 11 am. At that time, in addition to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the British and French Concession Police Department dispatching police to take care of order, there is also a foreign man who is enthusiastic about walking, Mr. A. Czech, who will prepare refreshments in the basketball hall on that day to provide for the male and female athletes and staff. In the past two days, the Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Wen donated a large silver cup, the Universal Insurance Company donated a huge silver tripod, Mr. A. Czech donated four large and small silver cups, the Fuchang Gift Bureau donated two silver shields for men and women, and the Sanduo Company donated a large silver shield. It is said that there are still elderly cups, etc., that will be delivered soon. Staff members are requested to gather at the intersection of Tongfu Road at 7:30 am. Those who have not received ribbons are requested to obtain them from Lu Yutian that morning. The 13-mile route is as follows: Depart from the intersection of Tongfu Road, Jing'an Temple Road, Jing'an Temple Road, Quejisi Road, Bailinan Road, cross the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway to Zhoujiaqiao, south to Huobilan Road, Bahongqiao Road, Haige Road, pass Nanyang University to Xiahui Road, turn to Yaozhujiao Road, Beidang Road, Lafayette Road, Albert Road, south to Fululi Road, Xuehuali Road, Kangti Road, north to Saposai Road, Laorenfu Road, and end at the Chinese Athletics Field. Regarding the Sino-German Art Exhibition: The National Art Community Plans to Issue a Statement to the German Government That the Current Works Are Not Representative of Chinese Culture

(Nanjing, 10th Dispatch) Wang Qi, Li Yishi, Liang Dingming and more than ten others, due to the request to postpone the Sino-German Art Exhibition, the government has not made a concrete expression. They plan to jointly send a telegram to the German government on behalf of the national art community, stating that the works carried by Liu Haisu, which are said to be for exhibition, have not been widely solicited or publicly reviewed, and are not sufficient to represent Chinese culture. They are currently seeking co-signatories. (Nanjing, 10th Dispatch) Wang Qi, Liang Dingming, and others believe that the Sino-German Art Exhibition is of great importance to China's cultural standing. They had requested the authorities to publicly solicit submissions and postpone the event. On the 10th, newspapers reported that Liu Haisu was scheduled to take the exhibits to Europe on the 14th. According to Wang Qi's statement to reporters, Liu rashly set off without waiting for the government to resolve the matter. His colleagues are determined not to remain silent and will jointly send a telegram to the German government and publish it in European newspapers, exposing that the exhibits carried by Liu this time have not been publicly solicited or reviewed and are not sufficient to represent Chinese culture.

The Citywide Boy Scouts Will Hold Their Fifth Annual Inspection and Camporee Today

▲A Total of 60 Troops and 3,487 People Participating in the Inspection ▲209 Camp Tents with 267 People Participating in the Camporee ▲Pan Gongzhan, Tong Xingbai, and Nine Others Serve as the Presidium

The Municipal Boy Scout Council originally scheduled to hold the Fifth Annual Inspection and Camporee in the city center on Double Ten Day. Due to the muddy ground after the site was used, the event was postponed. It has now been scheduled to take place in front of the new municipal government building today (the 11th) for a total of three days, with more than 3,500 participants. The detailed information is as follows:

Number of Participants

Participants who underwent inspection included 41 groups belonging to the council, as well as 19 schools, including the Shanghai Municipal Girls' High School, Shanghai Girls' High School, Dazhong Middle School, Datong Affiliated Middle School, Danhua Middle School, Shangwen Elementary School, Yucai Elementary School, Linyin Elementary School, YMCA Middle School, Peicheng Elementary School, Tonghui Elementary School, Liuyun Elementary School, Jingye Elementary School, Zijin Elementary School, Hub North Elementary School, Hu East Elementary School, Yangzheng Elementary School, Chuangzhi Elementary School, and the Huacheng Workers' Children's School. March-past, B. Parade; (8) Chairman's report; (9) Admonition; (10) Singing the Boy Scout song; (11) Cheers; (12) Submerging; (13) Ceremony completed (music played).

Spring and Autumn

"Existing Since Ancient Times" and "Also Existing in Foreign Countries"

— Nineteen

There are two very common sayings in China now: one is "existing since ancient times," and the other is "also existing in foreign countries." It seems that these are two parallel tracks, and everything either tends to this or tends to that. Therefore, although it is clear that cold pork is no longer fortunate enough to be eaten, the Confucius Temple must still be preserved; otherwise, it would be "cutting off the sage!" This is because the Confucius Temple has "existed since ancient times." "Miss" and Miss, "sorry" and "borrow" (Sorry), are originally one and two, and two and one; however, if you want to say it more beautifully, then Miss should be renamed "Miss," and "sorry" should be changed to "borrow." This is too much because the two terms "Miss" and "borrow" "also exist in foreign countries." A few examples are enough to prove that the two phrases "existing since ancient times" and "also existing in foreign countries" should not be underestimated.

Mencius said: "If a country has no external troubles, it will perish." Correct. This is indeed not only "existing since ancient times" but also "also existing in foreign countries." Ten years of accumulation and ten years of training, Goujian finally conquered Wu. This is "existing since ancient times." In the Franco-Prussian War, France ceded Alsace and Lorraine to Prussia, but in less than fifty years, a great war broke out in Europe, and France was finally able to recover its lost territory in 1918. This is "also existing in foreign countries." Because of this, the country will perish even if it has no external enemies; then, even if the land is lost, everyone can rest assured that it can be recovered in ten or dozens of years, so why worry! When Hu Liefu is mentioned, everyone wants to gnash their teeth; however, "traitors" have "existed since ancient times." Just take the Ming Dynasty: "In June of the sixteenth year of Hongwu, eighteen barbarian ships invaded Xiaohuosai, Jinxiang, and the government troops defeated them. The following year, Hu Weiyong falsely sent Li Wang from Luzhou to act as an envoy to return, and Lin Xian... came with the monk Ruyue to present giant candles containing gunpowder and weapons, plotting rebellion: by the time it arrived, Weiyong was executed, and the court punished his rebellious party, imposing extreme penalties on Xian." See Gu Tinglin's Book on the Benefits and Diseases of the World's Kingdoms, Overseas Barbarians. Hu Weiyong and Lin Xian were both "traitors": isn't this "existing since ancient times"? Therefore, "traitors" should never be made to be.

"Control" is "Control," and "prize coupons" are "Lottery." There are many more foreign fresh terms that are gradually or will be coming in a steady stream. Although this cannot be said to have "existed since ancient times," it "also exists in foreign countries." "Existing since ancient times" is enough to convince people; moreover, since it "also exists in foreign countries," there is naturally nothing more to say.

Four Company Commanders in the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 18: Tenderly Passing Tea to Comfort the Husband, Hastily Leaving the Village with a Forced Smile Bidding Farewell to the Family

Even though half of his face was covered, Zhao Ziqiang could still recognize him. He couldn't help but shout, "Isn't that Old Liu from the east end of the street?" Old Liu jumped off the cart, dropped the whip in his hand, and bowed deeply to him with both hands, saying, "Company Commander Zhao, look at this, what should I do? My whole family is counting on my cart and these two animals, running back and forth between the city and Haidian. Now I've brought them all here, what should I do? I thought you didn't recognize me. I wanted to call out to you several times, but I was afraid of committing a crime and didn't dare to call out. It's good that you recognize me. I still have an eighty-year-old mother at home, you know." As he spoke, he simply knelt down and kowtowed to Zhao Ziqiang three times. Zhao Ziqiang saw his eyes rolling, and tears were about to fall. He reached out and helped him up. He was just about to say something and then discuss it further, but when he looked behind him, there were four more large carts that had been pulled over, following closely behind. Naturally, each cart also had a driver sitting on it, all staring at Old Liu with wide eyes. So he hardened his heart and said with a stern face, "You're talking nonsense. If I could let you go, why would I have brought you here? You'll come with us, and it won't be a loss for you. One day of travel, one day of money." Old Liu kowtowed twice and was criticized for talking nonsense. He had no choice but to hold back his tears, stand up, and sit back on the cart to drive. Zhao Ziqiang led the quartermaster and simply rode back to the camp in the five carts. When he walked back to the company headquarters, he ran into Tian Qing, who laughed, "You're better off than me. You went home to see your lover." Zhao Ziqiang didn't say anything and sighed heavily. Tian Qing laughed, "What's wrong? Did your mother-in-law have anything to complain about?" Zhao Ziqiang said, "Ah! That's not it, but..." As he spoke, he took off his military cap with his left hand and stroked his head with his right hand, indicating his hesitant and helpless expression. (237)

Homesickness and Urban Ailment

— Wei Jing

No one can avoid feeling isolated and lonely when first stepping into this city, cursing everything around them, everything that seems to be mocking them. And thinking of home twelve times a day. Indeed, everyone who first steps into this city has this symptom, which is said to be called "homesickness."

"Homesickness" is not an incurable disease, nor is it as serious as "lovesickness," and there is no need to ask a traditional Chinese medicine doctor for a prescription or a Western medicine doctor for an injection. It will not involve life and death. The only treatment is to use your spare time to pursue a place to "relieve your boredom." In the city, places to "relieve your boredom" are more abundant and complete than anything else. Among them, the one that gets the brain rolling and the thumb pointing is naturally the "dance hall." In the dance hall, there are tempting faces and thighs, and intoxicating champagne and beer. Under the obscured bright electric lights, in the jazz sounds that are joyful without being lewd and mournful without being resentful, you will lose your entire soul, and you will be happy here and not think of Shu.

If you don't go to the dance hall, then please go to the cinema to relieve your boredom. Or go to the park, too. In the cinema, in the park, if you are lucky and have a good love star, then women will come after you without you chasing them. Even if you take a hundred steps back, if there are no women chasing you, then there are many opportunities in those places, if you are not Liu Xiahui or a man of Lu.

Amusement parks. Compared to dance halls, cinemas, and parks, they are naturally inferior, but as a place to "relieve your boredom," it is not necessarily a bad place. There, there is also everything that is charming and intoxicating, and the tempting ingredients are relatively stronger. And it is even more of a good medicine for those suffering from homesickness.

To put it more simply and easily, then strolling along a few bustling streets is already interesting enough, and especially at night, on those famous mysterious streets. On those mysterious streets, you can experience "exoticism." If you are interested and step into the coffee shop frequented by decadent Chinese poets, then you may realize what the so-called "southern style" is all about.

These, these, are enough to cure your unshakeable "homesickness," but the incurable "urban ailment" is also beginning to bury your soul in the grave.

A Record of Mr. Liang from Guangdong

— Jinzi

First of all, I want to declare that I am a "backward person of the times" who believes in the theory of cause and effect; but even if the times abandon me, the facts that happen before my eyes are pouring over to my way of thinking, and so I grasp the theory of cause and effect more firmly. If you don't believe me, please read below丨

There is a Cantonese person surnamed Liang, whose name will not be published for the time being. However, he works at the Shanghai Two-Road Administration, and it is not difficult to inquire. Although he is already very old, his appetite is very strong. Cantonese people originally like to eat the most, and they like to eat strange things, such as three snakes and rice worms, which people in other places dare not touch, but they love to eat them like their lives. Liang's appetite is even stronger than that of ordinary Cantonese people, and his income is not low, so he is wholeheartedly trying to study eating as much as possible, especially raw turtle meat, which is the most special. Turtle meat is also eaten by many locals, and it goes without saying that Cantonese people eat it even more, but it is probably rare to eat it raw like Liang. The method is to first feed a turtle until it is very fat and full, and then wash it clean with water. Liang then grabs the turtle with one hand and holds a knife with the other. As the knife flashes, the turtle's head falls off at the neck, and Liang turns it upside down and puts his mouth on the turtle's broken neck, sucking its fresh blood with force. At this time, the turtle is not completely dead, and its four legs are desperately moving and scratching outside the shell, just corresponding to the clicking sound coming from Liang's mouth. By the time he has finished sucking the turtle's blood, the turtle's legs are no longer moving. Let's not talk about this for now.

Just say that this spring, rape flower turtles were on the market, and Liang couldn't help but have a strong appetite and wanted to eat a big meal.

Unexpectedly, a boil suddenly grew on his own neck, festering unbearably. He asked a doctor to see it, who said it was the most dangerous "carbuncle on the head," and the only way to save it was to have surgery. So Liang was hospitalized for surgery. Unexpectedly, when the doctor made a light cut, his head fell off with the knife. It was cut off at the neck, and fresh blood gushed out, just like the situation he had inflicted on the turtle.

That's how the matter ended.

Tendency of Film Style

— Li Jingxian

Although film in our China has only been around for more than ten years, it has undoubtedly become our most powerful weapon.

Its stylistic changes, searching for the traces of its evolution from the transitions, can be found in these: 丨丨

In the beginning, of course, it could not escape the childish elements of "farce" and "hooliganism." Later, some people knew that it could be used to open up people's wisdom. Thus, it was regarded as a work of popularizing civilian education, but the style inevitably had some regrets similar to the method of preaching. Later, the tide of martial arts was like a torrent raging in the silver sea, and unfortunately, the waves of gods and monsters even mixed into the heavy siege of this climax, causing the bright silver sea to be disturbed, causing shadows to become pitch black.

But this shadow soon dissipated its trace, and the tendency of Chinese film style entered a new realm.

This realm is tending towards our masses. It will no longer be a simple entertainment product for people, but will go further to shout, awaken, and awaken this group of lambs who are lost and cannot find a way out for our masses who are trapped in suffering.

It is said that the new film "Iron Plate Red Tears Record" by Mingxing New Film has a picture composed of bold lines. These lines can fully depict the crimes of the past warlords who poisoned the people with exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, and the tense posture of the revolutionary seeds brewing on the eve of the outbreak.

Remember, this stylistic tendency is standing on our side.

Fashion Special Issue, Issue 10

Farewell to Readers

— Editor

This publication has been published for ten issues since September 9th. In these short two months, we ask ourselves if we have achieved anything significant; but we have at least achieved two goals: first, to promote domestic clothing materials, and second, to popularize clothing. We certainly dare not boast that this fashion special issue has much ability and effect; but we also do not shy away from the fact that in these two months, domestic clothing has indeed become more popular due to the promotion of this publication. Also, although we have also created novel and hygienic styles of clothing, the avoidance of extremely luxurious decorations on cheongsams (popular clothing) and only trimming one side, and the lack of lace on the inside of the robes, etc., have also become very popular. This can reduce the burden of tailoring costs by a considerable amount.

We deeply feel that the clothing expenses in each family are probably 70% to 80% for women; we also believe that if all the ladies understand that domestic clothing materials are so cheap and of good quality, then the annual leak of 300 million yuan of foreign goods can be greatly reduced: at the same time, we also hope that the clothing of the masses should meet the three principles of "economy," "hygiene," and beautification.

Now that the weather is cool, everyone has mostly prepared for winter clothes, so the colleagues want to take advantage of this period to make an end. It is not known whether they will continue to publish in the future if there is another opportunity? At the same time, this publication has reached an agreement with the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, Zhanghua Woolen Company, Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and Hongxiang Clothing Company, that if readers have any questions about clothing, they may write to any one of them and ask in detail, and they will definitely enthusiastically tell you everything you want to know, if the clothing materials are completely domestic.

This Week's Fashion Changes, Editor's Report

In this week, we can see in public places that many women's cheongsams are slightly shorter than before. The cheongsams of the past were so long that they dragged on the ground, and the hem was very dirty and would tear. Now, they probably only reach the ankles.

There is a coat style this year that is not only very new but also beautiful. A large pleat is made on the back, and a pleat is made on each side of the chest, and a pleat is also made on the lower left and right parts of the hem, so it is very comfortable to wear.

Recently, Mr. Wang Jingwei said that senior staff should wear mandarin jackets. So men's mandarin jackets are fashionable again, mostly made of domestic black georgette.

After Returning Home (Part 2)

— Shou Juan

For several days in a row, Madame acted like an inspector on the road, trying to find a Western suit material for her husband everywhere. One evening, she excitedly rushed home with a fairly large bag, gesticulating and saying to her husband, "Okay, okay, I've already gotten you a good material for a suit. You look at it, and I guarantee you'll be satisfied." As she spoke, she opened the bag and held a stack of smooth and lovely suit wools in both hands, sending them straight to Mr. C's eyes. Mr. C first glanced at it casually, and there was already a point of satisfaction on his face. Then he pinched it with two fingers, and there were three points of satisfaction on his face. Then he grabbed a corner of the material and rubbed his hands vigorously against each other. There were suddenly nine points of satisfaction on his face. Finally, he picked up the whole piece and held it in both palms, bouncing it up and down. There were twelve points of satisfaction on his face, and he shouted joyfully, "My love, my love! Where did you buy this material? I think it must be from a famous German factory. No other country can make such authentic goods. I've been looking for it for a long time and couldn't find it, but it just fell into your hands. It really didn't take any effort at all." Madame smiled and said, "I knew you would be satisfied when you saw material like this. I got it from a German friend." Mr. C clapped his hands and cheered, "Isn't that right? Isn't that right? I'm still a German expert. I knew it was German goods at a glance. If I'm wrong, you can just gouge out my eyes." When Madame heard this, she started to giggle and laugh, laughing so hard that she leaned forward and backward, and tears came out. Mr. C hurriedly said, "What are you laughing at? I mean what I say. If I'm wrong, anyone can gouge out my eyes." Madame wiped her tears as she laughed and nodded repeatedly, saying, "Okay, okay, you sit still and don't move. I'll gouge out your eyes." As she spoke, she took a small knife from the table and walked up to Mr. C, but then she suddenly put the knife down, lowered her head, and said with a smile, "Darling, I'm not going to gouge out your eyes. I'm still going to pry open your Western-obsessed mind. You should know that this material is not German goods at all. It's actually a domestic product of your Republic of China." Mr. C said in surprise, "How so? Can we Chinese make such authentic suit wools? No matter what, I can't believe it." Madame said, "If you dare to talk back again, then I will not only gouge out your eyes, but also cut off your tongue. To tell you the truth, this is indeed your domestic product. I bought it from a wool shop on Nanjing Road that makes fashionable dresses with dark brown mei-chang crepe, lotus leaf sleeves with similar cuffs, circular waist openings, and exposed white arms. It is extremely dignified and beautiful for plump people to wear this.

It was bought from a wool shop at the intersection of East Road. According to my partners, it is made by the Zhanghua Woolen Textile Company, called Jin Yangmao brand Zhanghua wool, and the goods are both high-quality and cheap. If you don't believe me, I can accompany you to see it. There are many similar things on display in that shop, and the name of that shop is also called Zhanghua." Mr. C was still unwilling to believe it easily. He carefully looked at the material again, pinched it, rubbed it, and bounced it up and down, saying with surprise and joy, "This is really strange. We hopeless Chinese can make such authentic suit wools. It's both clean and fine, and the color is good, and the texture is firm. It's really comparable to authentic German goods. From now on, I can only be considered a blind person, and I will no longer dare to underestimate any of our domestic goods. And I want to make an oath that from today onwards, I will love China with a hundred and twenty percent sincerity and love our Chinese domestic goods."

So Mr. C was cured of his deep-rooted Western obsession by his wife and transformed into a passionate patriot and a member who loves to use all domestic goods.

Film star Ms. Zhu Qiuhen photographed wearing winter casual wear made of Hongxin Factory's new butterfly velvet

Principles of Beauty and Fit in Clothing

— Qin Zhi

Since our country's Xuanyuan clan created clothing, more than four thousand years have passed, during which time there have been changes. Length, width, and narrowness have been repeatedly altered, truly because the way of clothing must both follow the evolution of the times to create aesthetic styles, and also align with the original purpose of hygiene to seek tailoring that fits the body. This is not merely for covering the body and keeping warm. In recent times, science has flourished, and human intelligence has also increased accordingly. In all things, we seek to promote benefits and eliminate drawbacks, discarding the crude and embracing the new. Moreover, clothing is the foremost of the four necessities of life, and striving for its reform is even more important than other items. Therefore, European and Western countries devote themselves to research on clothing, sparing no effort. The dressmakers, in particular, compete with each other in ingenuity and strength. Looking back at our country's dressmakers, they only know to follow old methods, lack specialized knowledge, and have even less relevant experience, let alone aesthetic sense and fit. They hardly know whether our clothing is suitable or not, primarily depending on the quality of its tailoring, with the cost of the materials being secondary. Consider expensive materials like silk and satin. If the tailoring is not done properly, it will not only lose its beauty but also evoke aversion. Conversely, inexpensive materials like homespun cloth, if tailored properly, will not only enhance beauty but also align with the original purpose of hygiene. It is like a chef cooking vegetables. Regardless of whether they are garden vegetables or plain dishes, as long as the cooking is done properly – what should be salty, what should be sweet, what should have added fragrance, and what should have added spice – the result can surpass even the most exquisite delicacies. Conversely, if rare delicacies are not cooked properly, the raw materials may be expensive, but the taste will be like chewing wax, which is a pity. Applying this analogy, how important is tailoring to clothing? The Hongxiang Company specializes in making various styles of women's clothing, studying the ancient styles passed down from previous generations and extensively researching the improved new methods of Europe and the West, discarding the crude and preserving the essence. It also hires specialized talent and applies methods of borrowing and contrasting, along with the study of color schemes. Regardless of whether the material is silk or cloth, they can all handle it with ease. Now, because the company is dedicated to serving the women's community, it is happy to answer any inquiries about domestic clothing materials.

Long-Term Resistance and the Cloth Clothing Movement

Recently, it was heard that the Japanese anticipate a large number of orders from countries around the world from 1936 to 1937. They are exciting the national sentiment, calling on people to save money in preparation to support the great war for three years. Our country's wounds have not yet healed. Once a world war breaks out, both finances and talent will be exhausted. What ability do we have to participate? Therefore, during this time of national crisis (assumed to be five years), we should strive to economize on all material resources. Even wealthy families wearing cloth clothing to save financial resources is no great loss. Everyone has the heart of resisting to the death, and everyone has the thought of wiping out humiliation and avenging. We can seek the fortune of heaven and strive for one in ten thousand survival. Even today, a strong nation like Japan still has a National Products Promotion Committee that investigates national purchases of foreign goods and finds that there are still over 140 types. After research, they found that domestic products can replace 120 types of foreign goods. There are still over 20 types for which there is nothing to replace. Why must our people prefer foreign goods for everyday necessities like clothing? If they are not out of their minds, how can they bear to do this? This is the argument for wearing cloth clothing for long-term resistance.

The suffering of the rural areas has reached its extreme. After the floods, there followed the ravages of war. Fortunately, last year was uneventful, but the prices of rice and wheat were low, and selling them was worthless. However, the payment of rent and taxes remained the same, and the collection of debts remained the same. People want to sell their cultivated land, but there are no buyers. They want to pawn all their belongings, but pawnshops are closed. Strong and violent men become bandits. At best, there are petty thefts. At worst, there are robberies and kidnappings for a living. Young women all go to Shanghai to work as maids, struggling to make a living. The fields are barren, families are ruined, and people die. What they witness is heartbreaking, beyond what pen and ink can describe. Now, the purpose of the Homespun Cloth Movement is to directly promote domestic products and resist enemy goods, indirectly relieving the rural areas. Spinning and weaving were originally sideline occupations for rural farmers during leisure time. All parts of our Jiangsu province are capable of doing so. However, because of the popularity of foreign cloth, and the fact that the enemy country seized the sales channels for homespun cloth in the three northeastern provinces, handmade production is almost non-existent. Now, if we vigorously promote it, and 400 million people wear cloth clothing during the national crisis, then if each person uses four bolts of homespun cloth per year, there will be a sales volume of 1.6 billion bolts. If the weaving cost of homespun cloth is calculated at 30 cents per bolt, the farmers will have an income of 480 million yuan. From where could the government find such a large sum of money to relieve the rural areas? Moreover, spinning and weaving skills are familiar to rural women, so there is no need to hire craftsmen to teach them. Farm families already have spinning and weaving equipment, so there is no need to raise a huge sum of money to start the business. Each family can increase sideline production while still raising children and managing household affairs, without the suffering of leaving their hometowns to live the factory life of going out in the morning and returning in the evening. What benefit is greater than this in promoting homespun cloth? However, promotion is not difficult; sales channels are. The power of one person is limited, so we must rely on 400 million people to make a vow to wear cloth clothing to succeed. Whenever there are disasters in various places, and relief funds are raised, all our compatriots enthusiastically contribute because it benefits the disaster victims. Now, if we wear cloth clothing, we can resist inferior goods, express patriotism, and the cloth we buy will be funds to relieve the rural areas. Why would people not be happy to do so? I hope that patriotic men and women will not only wear cloth clothing themselves but also widely encourage their compatriots to happily buy cloth clothing. Wearing one more cloth clothing is like saving one more farm family's life. This is why saving the rural areas is even more important than promoting cloth clothing.

During this period of promoting domestic goods, patriotic people are all advocating and publicizing domestic products. The great river does not refuse small streams, and the peaks of the mountains are based on the soil. Rural homespun cloth is closely related to handmade sideline occupations. If its use is promoted, it may be a way to resist inferior goods.

My Thoughts on Clothing

— Pan Hengruo

Clothing should be clean and not ostentatious, and we should avoid extravagance. Clothing is the biggest expense for us women. Ms. Li, who lives next door to the east, spends about four to five thousand yuan a year on clothing materials. Ms. Wang, who lives next door to the west, spends more than one thousand yuan a year just on tailoring fashionable clothes. This situation is jaw-dropping. In fact, a person needs beautiful behavior, a beautiful disposition, beautiful words, and beautiful knowledge. As for clothing, as long as it is domestic, elegant, and always able to show beauty, why must we buy foreign goods, wear European and American silk and satin, buy foreign patterns, and then make it into Liang-style clothing? In my opinion, the key points of clothing are cleanliness, simplicity, elegance, and especially durability. My annual clothing expenses are only about fifty yuan. What suits my taste best are silk and satin – domestic silk and satin, which are the national essence of China, are cheap and of good quality, and are welcomed by everyone. Products from Mayar Silk Mill are enough to meet our needs.

The other is cloth – domestic cloth, which is even more the national soul of China, is simple and elegant, and clean, is what everyone is happy to wear. The new dyeing and weaving products from Zhixia are suitable for everyone to wear. During this year of national goods, if we continue to promote it, it can become popular throughout the country.

Besides being happy to wear silk and satin clothes in the summer, I still wear cloth clothes in the three seasons of autumn and winter. Therefore, Hongxin Cloth and Mayar Silk are my loyal customers. I hope my sisters will all try it out.

Wireless Weekly

From a Three-Tube Radio to a Three-Tube Transmitter

— Zhu Ziyuan

If you already have a three-tube radio with one-stage detection and two-stage low-frequency amplification, then it is not difficult to convert it into a three-tube transmitter, and the additional parts required are not many. If you are interested in transmission, just take it and modify it, changing from a radio to a transmitter. Wouldn't that be interesting?

Below is an introduction to the modification method. For the sake of clarity, only the triode is taken as an example. If it is an AC device, it can also be modified in the same way, with minor differences.

The circuit diagram and explanation are as follows:

CC1 is a .0005 microfarad variable capacitor

C2 is a .003 microfarad fixed capacitor

C3 is a .00025 microfarad fixed capacitor

L is a tuning coil

RFC is a high-frequency choke coil, using a 2-inch diameter rubber tube, wound with 28-gauge silk-covered wire for 200 turns.

LFC is a low-frequency choke coil, which can be replaced by a low-frequency transformer with a broken primary coil (use its secondary) circuit diagram

R is a 10,000-ohm fixed resistor

Rr is a 6-ohm variable resistor

T is a low-frequency transformer

T' is a modulation transformer, which can be replaced by a low-frequency transformer.

D is a microphone battery, from 4.5 volts to 6 volts.

It can be said that the above parts can all be found in the radio, but the microphone and the 10,000-ohm fixed resistor R need to be purchased. This magazine has already published a method of making a gramophone pickup using a stethoscope. Readers can also imitate it according to the method. As for the wiring and arrangement, they are the same as the installation method of a radio. The RFC should not be placed in the magnetic field of L. It is best to keep it away or at a right angle.

The manufacturing method of L is as follows: Use a 4-inch long and 2.5-inch diameter rubber tube, leaving half an inch empty at each end, and wind 30 turns with 18-gauge wire (10 turns per inch), and adjust with a sliding key. The sliding rod is connected to A+ (K in the figure). The wavelength is approximately from 150 to 200 meters.

After assembly, you can use a radio suitable for 150 to 200 meters to listen nearby to correct your own wavelength. However, be careful not to intrude into the broadcasting range. At the same time, to be careful, it is still best to register with the Ministry of Communications. I think the authorities will not necessarily disapprove of amateur experiments, right?

As for the adjustment method, this magazine continuously publishes Mr. Luo Jingyu's "Shortwave Transmitter Adjustment Method and Steps". Readers can read it carefully.

Further Discussion on Remedying Unstable Power Supply Voltage

— Wei Xin Su

The instability of power supply voltage has a significant impact on radios and should not be ignored. Excessive voltage will shorten the life of vacuum tubes, rectifiers, and filters, and may even cause damage. However, insufficient voltage not only weakens the volume and diminishes selectivity but also harms the vacuum tubes. When the filament temperature is too low, arcing often occurs.

In a previous issue of this magazine, the author suggested connecting a step-down transformer in series with the radio's power supply transformer to adjust the voltage. Although this method is simple and economical, it requires constant manual adjustments and is not suitable for general radio users. Therefore, two other types of automatic voltage regulators are introduced below.

Voltage regulators available on the market are made of variable resistors placed in a perforated metal cylinder. When encountering excessive voltage, their resistance increases with temperature. When encountering normal or low voltage, their resistance is very low. Although this type of regulator can suppress excessive voltage, it is powerless against voltage drops. Now, according to the method in Figure 1, if the lowest voltage in a certain area is 100V, you can connect a door-bell transformer with an input of 110V and an output of 12V in series, so that this 12V is added to the 100V to raise the voltage to 112V, and after passing through the regulator, you can get 110V. This device can automatically adjust even if the power supply voltage returns to normal or becomes excessive. As the voltage increases, its resistance also increases, keeping the voltage supplied to the radio close to 110V. It should be noted that the ampere rating of the door-bell transformer used above must not be less than the ampere required by the radio.

Figure 1 Figure 2

A voltage compensator is a specially designed step-up autotransformer as shown in Figure 2. When the voltage drops, this step-up transformer can raise the voltage to restore it to normal. Part C in the figure functions slightly below the magnetic permeability saturation knee of the core. If the voltage is excessive, the saturation of part C of the core will also increase, so a strong part of the magnetic lines passes through part D through the gap, which causes the B coil to generate the opposite polarity and eliminate the excess voltage. The author is not clear whether this voltage compensator can be bought in stores in Shanghai. In the United States, there is a product from Sola Corp. with an input voltage from 95V to 135V, which can supply 100 watts of power.

The Method of Making a Tungar Tube Charger

— Yizhi

Friends who have storage batteries will feel that it is troublesome and expensive to carry the bulky storage batteries to the electrical material store for charging. Who doesn't want to have a charger of their own, just plug the plug into the light wire, connect the positive and negative wires on the charger, and remove it after it is fully charged? How convenient! However, buying a charger costs more than fifty or sixty yuan. Some people are afraid of being limited by their finances, and some are reluctant to spend so much money, so they can't charge it themselves, and they have to suffer every month by moving the battery back and forth. I am also one of the sufferers. I often complain when I want to charge it. Therefore, I decided to make a charger myself. After more than ten days of work, I made a Tungar tube charger. It cost a total of more than 20 yuan, and the results are pretty good. If compared with foreign goods, the effect is the same, but the money is saved by more than half. It is now a time to promote domestic goods, economic patriotism, and save a sum of money, which will be sent to foreigners. Moreover, after doing it myself, I gained an experience, and if it is damaged, I can repair it myself. Isn't it a very worthwhile thing to do? I think there must be many friends who like to play with wireless and want to make this charger, so I will introduce the manufacturing method (because of space limitations, I cannot explain it in detail, I can only select the essentials to describe: if you have any questions, please submit a letter to this magazine and forward it to me, so that I can give instructions and conduct joint research.)

The materials needed for this Tungar Charger are listed below:

Tungar Tube One

110V 40W Carbon lamp One

Transformer One (self-made or modified)

Ammeter One

Resistor One

Screw lamp holder Two

Plug and socket Three pairs

17-gauge double yarn-wrapped wire More than two pounds

16-gauge double yarn-wrapped wire Eighty feet

German Silver Wire Thirty feet, etc.

Except for the Tungar tube, carbon filament lamp, and ammeter, the other items listed above cannot be made by oneself, the rest can be bought and configured.

Tungar tubes commonly used on the market are produced by General Electric Company of America. It has two advantages: (1) durable, (2) good efficiency. The types depend on the current capacity, divided into: (1) 2 amps (2) 6 amps. Now we buy a 2-amp type that is enough. The 2-amp Tungar form is shown in Figure 1

Figure 1

There is a mercury-like substance coated inside this tube. The lower part is slightly transparent, and you can see the filament and the screen. The filament is made of tungsten wire, and the screen is made of carbon. When you buy it, the filament is slightly shiny; the surface of the screen is very smooth and has no black spots.

Ammeter If you already have a volt-ampere meter, or a milliampere meter with a shunt, you can use it without buying it.

Transformer If it is used on an AC generator with 60-70 watts of power, it can be used. Just disassemble and rewind the coil to complete it. If you want to make one yourself, buy about 4 pounds of 4 1/2" x 1 1/2" silicon steel sheets. Prepare the iron sheets, and then make two winding frames that are fitted on the iron sheets, and you can start winding. (To be continued)

Random Musings on Radio (4)

— Wei Yan

(On the current status of the broadcasting industry in China)

XHAA, a radio station affiliated with the Chinese and Western Pharmacy, is known for its high-quality programming, with more academic programs than any other station. Recently, it has added morning exercises and movie reviews, which show its commitment to promoting sports and culture. However, the amount of advertising on the station is truly annoying. On average, there are several long advertisements for every half side of a record. Sometimes, when the mood strikes, they even insert advertisements while broadcasting records, which makes people feel dizzy and disoriented. If it is a special program, there will be more than ten advertisements at a time, which makes people sigh in disbelief. I am not against radio stations including advertisements in their programs, but there should be an appropriate amount of advertising. Too much advertising will make listeners switch to other stations, and the effectiveness of the advertisement will be zero. I think it is best to insert some advertisements after the end of one program and before the start of the next program. The number of advertisements can be increased at a time, but the time should not be too long. The wording should be concise and not repetitive. In this way, listeners will not switch the channel because they are eagerly awaiting the next program. (The Huamei and Yadong stations, etc., insert a short advertisement after each record, which we consider to be the most effective.)

XMHA, a broadcasting station established by Westerners in Shanghai, also has four or five stations, and their power is very large. Among them, the Western Huamei Broadcasting Station is the most popular with listeners for its long hours of Western music from 7:00 am to 12:30 pm every day. It is said that the pitch of their broadcasting machine can be controlled at any time, so the sound waves emitted are very pleasant to listen to.

Common Sense

— Huang Jiancun

(18) Overview of Vacuum Tubes (2)

(C) (B)

Tetrode: What distinguishes a tetrode from a triode is that the former has one more grid, that is, it is composed of a screen grid, a filament, and two grids. As shown in the figure above, (a) is the symbol used for tetrodes. In the figure, the one close to the filament is called the inner grid, and the one close to the screen grid is called the outer grid. Because of the different uses of these two inner and outer grids, tetrodes are divided into two types: screen grid tubes and space charge grid tubes. (b) The figure shows the structure and connection method of a space charge grid tube. In the figure, F is the filament, SCG is the space charge grid, CG is the control grid, and P is the screen grid. The space charge grid is connected to a positive voltage, and its function is to offset the negative electric field of space electrons to reduce the screen voltage. Originally, electrons emitted by the filament are distributed in the vacuum tube. These electrons form a negative electric field in the tube, which is the negative electric field of space electrons. In a triode, because of the existence of a negative electric field, it cannot be used unless the screen voltage is increased. However, the tetrode has another device to offset this negative electric field, which can reduce the screen voltage to increase its effectiveness. (c) The figure shows the structure and connection method of a screen grid tube. Its outer grid is used as the screen grid SG. The only difference from figure (b) is this point. In addition to offsetting the negative electric field of space electrons, the function of the screen grid is to reduce the internal capacitance of the tube to eliminate the drawbacks of its self-oscillation. The reason why tetrodes are particularly suitable for high-frequency amplifiers lies in this. Although there are two types of tetrodes mentioned above, because the function of the screen grid tube is superior, the screen grid tube is more used today, while the space charge grid tube is almost eliminated.
